thou haſt made true calcination encreſyng waſtyng moyſture radycall tyll thy baſe ofter ſubtylyatyon wyll lyghtly flow wex uppon mettall lowſe hyt wyth thy vegetable menſtruall tyll thou oyle thereof whych hym revyvyd men myght ſee ſo together may cyrculate y ſay oyle vegetable menſtruall ether ſo labour exuberate made crafte stone celeſtyall nature ſo fyrye yt call baſelysk otherwyſe cokatryſe baſe red whyte aurum potabile thus y made gold comyn calcynat tyncture whych wyll vade baſe drawen wyth menſtrue circulate naturall calcynatyon muſt algate made ere thy gold dyſſolved pryncypall fyrſt intente calcyne whych ſo bent fro thys hard scyence withdraw theyre hond till calcyning better underſtonde ſuch calcynyng theyre bodyes ſhent whych mynyſheth moyſture stone therefore bodyes powder brent dry askys tre bone ſuch calx wyll none moyſture multiply radycall calcynyng mynyſhyng none ſure ground trew calcynacyon woorch wyttyly kynde wyth kynde kynd kynde hath appetyble inclynacyon knoweth thys yn knowledge blynd may forth wander myſt doth wyth wynd woting never wyth perfytnes whereto lyght becauſe cannot conſeve word aryght joyne kynd kynd therefore reaſon y every burgeon anſwereth owne seed man begetteth man beaſt beaſt lykewyſe ferther thys trete need underſtond thys poynt yf thou wylt ſpede every thyng y fyrſt calcyned hys owne kynd thys well conſevyng frute thereyn solucyon yf thou dyd wyth water ſmall thyne erth glutyn whych loſyth take heede therefore potter loome make never neſh thy wome loome behold yt tempered y meane alſo thou hyt calcenate ever mynd loke sulphur worchyng invyſybly ferſely fyre brennyng body water dyſſolvyng body mynerall nyght fro darknes north parte call yet trow thou underſtandyſt utterly ſecrett phyloſopers dyſſolucion therefore erth y integrally yncynerat y water congelyd thys underſtond element ſo concatenat body fro hys fyrſt forme y alterate new forme y inducyd immediately nothyng wythout forme y utterly ſecret thee wyll dyſcloſe whych y ground ſecrets yf thou hyt know thou ſhalt loſe thy labour coſts great ſmall take hede therefore errour thou fall thyne erth leſſe thy water rather better solucyon ſhall thou ſee behold yſe water doth relent ſo hyt muſt water hyt ryght ſoe agayne water erth bent water thereby congelyd evermore phyloſophers whych ever bore every mettall ons water mynerall therefore wyth water ſhall caſt mountaynes bodyes lykewyſe laſt bodyes lekenyd convenyently mountaynes whych hygh planet name depenes therfore mercury turne kepe blame ſhall ye ſe nobyll game ſhall become powder ſoft wyth daylyght doth upryſe somer dyſporte wyth delyght thy warke ſhall becom parfyt whyte forth fro eſt ynto south aſſend ſett thou therein thy chayre fyre y harveſt y ſay end thys warke thyne owne deſyre ther ſhynyth son hys owne ſphyre eclyps y rednes wyth glory kyng rayne uppon mettalls mercury one glaſſe muſt done thys thyng lyke egg ſhape cloſyd well muſt know meſure fyryng whych unknowen thy warke y loſt ech dele lett never thy glaſſe hotter thow may feele ſuffer ſtyll thy bare hand holde dread loſyng philoſophers tolde yett doctryne furthermore intend beware thy glaſſe thou never opyn ne meve fro thy begynnyng tyll thou made end thou contrary thy warke may never cheve thus thys chapter whych y ſo breve taught thy trew solucion thyrd gate goe thys y separation third gate separacyon doth ech parte devyde ſubtill fro groce fro thyck thyn separacyon manuall look thou put aſyde pertaynyth folys whych lyttyll good wyn separacyon nature doth blyn makyng dyvyſyon qualytes elementall fyfth degree tyll turned erth y turnyd water black bloe water ayre whyte ayre y turned fyre element mo thys y made crafte stone grete delyte thys separacyon much muſt wryte separacyon y callyd phyloſophers dyffynycyon ſayd element tetraptatyve dyſperſyon thys separacyon fynde lyke fygure thus ſpoken prophet yn pſalmody god brought stone flud water pure hardyſt stone oyle abundantly ryght ſo precyoſe stone yf thou wytty oyle incombuſteble water thou ſhalt draw thereabout thou nedyſt cole blow thys wyth hete eſy meſuryng fyrſt wyth moyſt fyre wyth dry flewme pacyence owt drawyng thy nature wyttyly dry thyne erth tyll hyt thryſty calcenyng el thou laboryſt vayne make hyt drynke moyſture agayne separacyon thus muſt thou ofte tymes make thy matter dyvydyng part two symple fro groce thou take tyll erth remayne benethe color bloe erth y fyx abyde wo parte y spyrytuall fleyng thou muſt turne hem one thyng oyle water wyth water ſhall dyſtyll thorow help receve menyng kepe well thys two thou ſpyll thy wark lack dew cloſyng make thy stopell glas meltyng top thy veſsle together wyth yt phyloſopherlyke uſyd y hyt water wherwyth thou muſt renew thy stone looke thou dyſtyll afore thou warke wyth hyt oftentymes ſelfe alone thy ſyght thou ſhalt well wyt fro feculent feces hyt y quytt ſum men wyth saturne multeply subſtance defye dyſtyll hyt therfore tyll hyt clene thyn lyke water hyt ſhold hevyn color bryght ſhyne kepyng fygure ponderoſyte therwith dyd hermes moyſture hys tre wythyn hys glas made grow upryght wyth flower dyſcoloryd bewtyoſely ſyght thys water y lyke venemous tyre wherewyth myghty tryacle y wrought yt y poyſon moſt ſtronge yre ſtronger poyſon none thought att potecarys therfore oftyn yt y bought man ſhall hyt intoxycate tyme yt y medycyne elevate y tryacall trew hyt y poyſons moſt expulſyfe hys working doth mervells ſhewe preſervyng many deth lyfe loke thou meng yt wyth corroſyve cheſe hyt pure quick rennyng yf thou thereby wylt wynnyng y merveloſe thyng kynde wythout hyt may nought done therefore hermes calleth hyt hys wynde y flying fro sonn mone makyth stone flye wyth hyt sone revyvyng ded gevyng lyfe son mone husband wyfe whych yf craft made quick ther fatnes wyth water drawn ſo thyn dyſſevered thyke thou ſhould never bryng thys worke yf thou wylt ſpeed therefore wythout doubt reyſe thy byrd theyre neſt agayne bryng downe reſt water wyth water accord wyll aſſend spryt wyth spryt kynde whych exalted make dyſſend ſoe thou ſhalt devyde nature dyd bynde mercury eſſencyall turnyng wynde wythout whych naturall ſubtyll seperacyon may never compleat profytable generacyon help thee thys gate laſt secret wyll tell thee thy water muſt ſeven tymes sublymate ell ſhall kyndly dyſſolucyon putryfyyng ſhall thou none ſee like lyquyd stone dyſſeveryd chapter followyth ſecret conjunccion whych nature repugnant joyneth perfyt unyte ſo knyttyth none may fle whan fyre ſhall examynate soe together ſurely conjugate therfore phyloſophers geveth thys deffynycyon seyng thus conjunccion y nought ell dyſſeveryd qualytes copulacyon pryncypylls coequacyon tell ſome wyth mercury whych potecarys ſells medleth bodyes whych cannot dyvyde ther matter therefore ſtep aſyde unto tyme sowle separate clenſyd hys orygynall syn wyth water purely ſpyrytuallyzate thy trew conjunccion may thou never begyn therfore soule fyrſt fro body twyn corporall parte ſpyrytuall soule conjunccion ſhall cauſe perpetuall two conjunccions phyloſophers mentyon make groce body mercury y reincendat let hyt paſſe ſecond tent thou take ſayd y separacion celebrat whych party leſt whych leſt ſo collygate ſo promotyd unto moſt perfyt temperance never may among repugnance thus cauſyth separacion trew conjunccion water ayre earth fyre every element may lad ſo abyde ever thy deſyre done laborous clay myer temper thyke make thyn ſo drying thou ſhalt rather wyn manner thys conjunccion three fyrſt y callyd phyloſophers dyptative betwyxt agent patyent muſt male female mercury sulphure vive matter forme thyn thyke thryve thys leſſon wyll helpe thee wythout dowte conjunccion trewly bryng ſecond manner y called tryptative whych y conjunccion made thyngs three body sowle spyrit tyll ſtryve whych trynite muſt brought perfyt unyte sowle spyrit bond muſt ryght body sowle hym muſt knyt thy mynde let thys leſſon flyt thyrd manner alſo laſt fowre element together whych joynyth abyde tetraptative contently phyloſophers doth hyt call ſpecyally guydo de montayno whoſe fame goyth wyde therfore moſt laudable manner thys tyde conjunccion four element muſt aggregat dew proportion fyrſt whych aſonder ſeparat therefore lyke woman hath vaynes fyfteene man five act fecundyte requyryth conjunccion fyrſt mene muſt man sun hys water three nine hys wyfe whych three hym stone wythout ſuffer woman lygg alone ſhe hath conceyved man matryce ſhyt ſuch addyth evermore crude crude openyng theyr veſſells lettyng ther matter kele ſperme concevyd noryſh delude themſelfes ſpyllyth ther work every dele thou therefore lyſt well cloſe matryce noryſh ſeed wyth heat contynuall temperate thou wilt ſpede whan thy veſſle hath ſtond monyths five clowds clypſys paſſed ech one lyght apperen increaſe thy hete blyve tyll bryght ſhyneing whytneſſe thy stone may thou opyn thy glaſſe anone fede thy chyld whych y ybore wyth mylke mete ay moyſt dry ſo contemperate water erth hath recevyd impreſſyon whych never aſſunder may ſeperate ryght ſoe water erth hath given ingreſſyon together dwell hath made profeſſyon water erth hath purchaſyd retentive fower made one never ſtrive two thyngs entent doth hing dry moyſt whych contraryous two dry hyt moyſt fyxing bryng moyſt hyt geve lyquyfaccion erth unto thus contemperate may forth go temperament ſo thyk body y nother ſo thyn water wythout mys loſyng knyttyng therefore princypalls two thys hard scyence pole moſt pryncypall hyt pryncyples many mo ſhyneyng fanells whych ſhew ſhall proceed therefore unto another wall thys ſtrong caſtle wyſdome inner fyft gate thou may come putrefaction fift gate begynnyth chapter putrefaccion wythout whych pole ſede may multyply whych muſt done contynuall accyon hete body moyſt manually body ell may alterat naturally syth chryſt wytnes wythowt grayne whete dye ground encreſe may thou gete lykewyſe wythout thy matter putrefye may wyſe trewly alterate thyne element may devyded kyndly thy conjunccion perfytly celebrat thy labor therfore fruſtrate prevyte putrefying well underſtond ever thou take thys warke hond putrefaccyon may thus defyned phyloſophers ſayings y bodyes fleyng compound dyvyſyon thyngs thre kyllyng bodyes corrupcyon forth ledyng unto regeneratyon ablyng thyngs beyng erth wythowt dowte engendryd rotacyon hevyns aboute therfore ſeyd afore theyn element comyxt wyſely coequat thou keepe intemperat heate eſchuyng evermore violent hete never incynerat powder dry unprofytably rubyfycate powder blacke crowes byll wyth hete balne ell dounghyll tyme nyghts paſt nynty moyſt hete kepe fro eny thyng sone blacknes thow ſhalt eſpy draw faſt putrefying whych thow ſhalt many colers bryng perfyt whytenes wyth pacyence eſyly ſo thy ſede hys nature ſhall multeply make ech hawſe kyſſe lyke chyldren play downe ther ſherts fylyd wyth pyſſe lat woman waſh bound whych oftyn fayntnes wyll fall ſound dye laſt wyth chyldren go purgatory purg ther fylth orygynall lyttyll lyttyll encreſe ther paynys hete ay fyre lat never ceſe ſe thy fornace apt therfore whych wyſe men call athenor conſervyng hete requyryd moſt temperately whych water doth kyndly putrefy thys pryncypull ſpekyth sapyent guydo ſeyth rottyng dyeth compound corporall moryen mo upryſyth agayne regenerat sympill spyrytuall hete moyſture contynuall sperme wombe myght abydyng ſo ther ſhold therof frute upſpryng therfore begynnyng stonys thou take bery ech wyth wythin ther grave equally marryage betwyxt make ly together ſix wekys lat ther ſede conſevyd kyndly noryſh ſave ground ther grave ryſyng whych ſecret poynt doth many begyle thys tyme conceptyon wyth eſye hete abyde blacknes ſhowing ſhall tell dye together lyke lyquyd pyche tyde shall ſwell burbyll ſetyll putrefye shyning golors therin thou ſhalt eſpye lyke raynbow merveloſe unto ſyght water begynnyth dry upryght moyſt body hete noryſhyng temperate ingendryth blacknes fyrſt y kyndly commyxyon tokyn aſſygnate trew putrefying remember thys alter perfytly thou may myſſe thus gate blacknes thou muſt cum lyght paradyce whytenes yf thou wylt wyn fyrſt son hys upryſyng obſcurate shalbe paſſe water noyes flud erth whych hundred dayes contynuate fyfty away thys water yode ryght ſo water wyſe men underſtode shall paſſe thou wyth davyd may ſay abierunt ſicco fluminae bare thys away sone noe plantyd hys vyneyard whych really floryſhed brought forth graps anon whych ſpace thou ſhalt aſerd lykewyſe ſhall follow floryſhyng stone ſone uppon thyrty dayes overgone thou ſhalt graps ryght ruby red whych y adrop ulyfer red lede lyke sowles paynys tranſytory brought paradyce ever y yoyfull lyfe ſhall stone hys darknes purgatory purged joynyd element wythoute ſtryfe rejoyſe whytenes bewty hys wyfe paſſe fro darknes purgatory lyght paradyce whytnes elyxer gret myght thou may rather putrefaccyon wyn thys exampull thou take trew concluſyon ſecrett putrefaccyon reſtyth therein heart oke hath water contynuall infuſyon wyll ſone putrefy tell wythout deluſyon though yt water ly hundred yeres yet ſhold thou fynd ſound ever afore thou kepe hyt ſomtyme wete ſometyme dry thow many ſe tymber uſuall experyment proſſes tyme oke ſhall utterly putrefy ſoe lykewyſe accordyng entent sometyme tre muſt wyth son brent wyth water ſone muſt hyt kele thys menes thou ſhalt rottyng bryng hyt wele nowe wete nowe agayne dry grete hot agayne cold ſhall cauſe yt ſone putrefy ſo ſhalt thow bryng rottyng thy gold entrete thy body therfore thee told thy putrefying wyth hete ſo ſwyft leſt askys thou ſeke thy thryft therfore thy water erth thow draw make ſoule therwyth aſſend downe agayne erth hyt throw oft tymes ſo aſſend deſſend vyolent hete ſodayne cold defend thy glaſſe make thy fyre ſo temperat ſydys thy water never vytryfycate thou wyſe cheſing thy water medyll salt sulphure mene minerall whatſoever water clatter sulphure mercury mettall oylys water ſom men call fowlys byrd wyth namys many one becauſe folys themfelfs loſyng theyr ſyghts wyth odor ſmoks wakeyng nyghts clothes bawdy woryn thredebare men may ſmell multyplyers go fyle theyr fyngers wyth corroſyves ſpare theyr eye bleryd theyr chekys lene blood egg som tyll theyr thryſt gone devydyng element brekyng many pott multyplying ſherds yet hyt yt ſe theyr howſys y noble ſport fornaces glaſſys diver ſhape salt powder oyles water fort eloquently de materia prima clape yet fynde trewth hap mercury medle sulphur vyve wherein dote unthryve take red man hys whyte wyfe y ſpeciall thyng elixers two quinteſſence elixers lyfe hony celydony secundyns fayle fraunce wyn wonder thyng holy croſſe home wyll bryng yf king pryſoner take anon hys raunſome would make mervell yt y weſtminſter church whych theſe phyloſophers haunte syth ſo much ryches woorche make boſte avaunte drynkyng dayly wyne due taunte y made perfytly ons truly hyt lackyth yet many stonys folys doe folow tayle promotyd ryches wenyng wyll ye worſhyp avayle wyn london nobyll cyte wyth sylver macys ye may ſe sarjaunts awayting every owre men great honour sarjaunts ſekyth fro strete strete marchaunts goldſmyths leyeth watch well y wyth mete great advantage doe cache hunt theyr good powerte beſtad cache nobyll wold full glad sarjaunts areſt ther paukeners ſtuffed wyth parry ball wyth sygnetts seynt martynes leſt mony yt y pyſſyd wall led well befalls newgate ludgate tell becauſe ſhall ſafegard dwell y mony becom ſeyth one y myne ſeyth wyll ye ſuttell anon anſweryng excuſed may saying elyxers robbyd ell myght payd gold yf yt ten folde theyer creditor begyn flatter promyſyng worke agayne elyxers two ſhort ſpace dotyng merchaunts fayne let go ever vayne worke ſo long tyll laſt agayne pryſon caſt yf aske ryche ſey make fyne gold tynn ſey may ſurely ſwym dyche whych y upholden chyn ſtock therefore may nought wyn whych yf wold ſome worche fynyſh weſtmynſter churche ſome ſo devowte wyll dwell place may wythowten dowte lyft solace archedeacon y ſo full grace yf pleaſe hym wyth croſſe forſyth lyttyll menys loſſe ſyt wyne theſe monkys ſey many pound wolde god ſeyth one ſom myne hay hoe careaway lat cup go rounde drynk ſeyth another mene y founde maſter arte fayre promys makyth folys fayne ryall medycyne one upon twelve promys thereof whych could never themſelfe yet bryng abowte ſo god ſave beware ſuch phyloſophers man deprave whych helpyth theſe monkys ryches ſo wyth thread bare cowlys go abbot well ought cheryſh thys company tech hys monkys leve poverte go clothyd monyed relygyouſly dyd seynt benet eſchuyng ſuperfluyte eſyng alſo ponderoſyte theyr purſys wyth pound ſo aggravate whych phyloſophy allevyat lo ſo medlyth wyth thys rych company gret boſt ther wynnyng may make ſhall much ther phyloſophy tayle ape take beware therfore jeſus ſake medyll wyth nothyng gret coſt thou yt y loſt theſe phyloſophers whych ſpake afore medlyth blondryth wyth many thyng renuyng error lac trew underſtandyng lyke muſt lyke alway ferth bryng god hath ordeyned every kynde wold jeſus wold thys bere mynde wene nettyll roſe elder apple ſwete ala wyſe men ther good ſhold loſe truſtyng ſuch loſells mete whych ſeyth stone y trodyn fete makyth therfore vyle thyngs ſtyll tyll theyr howſys wyth ſtench fyll som never lernyd word scolys thynk reaſon underſtond phyloſophy phyloſophers nay folys therfore ther warkes provyth unwytty medyll wyth yf thou happy leſt wyth theyr flatteryng ſo tyll thou agre unto ther wyll spend thy mony away waſte geve every ſpeche credence fyrſt examyn grope taſte thou provyſt ſo put thy confydence ever beware grete expence yf thy phyloſopher lyve vertuoſely truſt better hys phyloſophy prove hym fyrſt hym oppoſe secretts stone whych yf know thou nedyth loſe medyll thou ferther let hym gone make never ſo pytyoſe mone fox fagg fayne wold faynyſt hys prey attayne yf anſwer ought clarke hyt hath provyd indede yf thou wylt helpe hym hys warke yf vertuoſe hold hyt mede wyll quyte yf ever ſpede thou ſhalt weete lytyll anon yf knowledge stone one thyng one glaſſe one furnace mo behold thys pryncypyll yf take yf lat hym go ſhall never thee rych man make trewly yt y better thou hym forſake wyth loſſe varyaunce manner dyſpleſaunce god fortune thys scyence doctrine whych told dyſcover yt whoever thee crave favor fere sylver gold none oppreſſor lecher boſter bold serve thy god helpe powre among yf thou thys lyfe lyſt continew long unto thy ſelfe thy ſecretts kepe ſynners whych hath god dred wyll caſt pryſon depe tyll thou tech hyt dede ſlander ſholde ſpryng ſprede thou dyd coyne wold ſey ſo undo ever aye yf thou teche thys conyng ſynfull levyng mayntayne hell therfore myght thy wonnyng god would diſdayne thow nought cowd thy ſelfe ſayne body soule may bothe ſave pece thy levyng thys chapter tought thou body muſt putrefy ſo guide thou cawght put duraunce loſſe vylanye doctryne therefore remember wyttyly paſſe forth toward syxth gate thys fyfthe y tryumphate congelation ſixt gate congelacyon nede much wryte yt y wyll fyrſt declare y ſoft thyngs induracyon colour whyte confyxacyon spyrits whych fleyng congele thee nedyth much care▪ element wyll knyt together ſone putrefaccyon kyndly done congelacyons made dyvers wyſe spyryts body dyſſolvyd water clere salt alſo dyſſolvyd ons twyſe congele fluxyble mater ſuch congelyng folys clatter ſome dyſsolvyth devydyng manually element congelyng powder dry ſuch congelyng y deſyre unto owers yt y contraryoſe congelacion dredyth fire yt muſt ever ſtond yt unctuos alſo hys tincture full bounteous whych ayre congelyd wyll relent water worke ſhent moreover congele ſo hard stone glaſſe cryſtall whych meltyth fuſyon ſo hyt lyke wax wyll melt anon wythouten blaſt beware deluſyon ſuch congelyng longyth concluſyon wyll flow ren water agen lyke salt congelyd laboryſt thou vayne whych congelacyon avaylyth u never dell hyt longyth multyplyers whych congele vulgarly yf thow therefore lyſt well syth thy medcyne ſhall never flow kyndly nether congele wythout thow fyrſt yt putrefye fyrſt purge fyx element stone tyll together congele flow anone matter y made parfyt whyte wyll thy spryte wyth body congelyd tyme thou muſt long reſpyte yer yt appere congelyd lyke pearles unto congelacyon glad ſee lyke graynys red blod rychyr worldly good erthly groſnes therefore fyrſt mortyfyed moyſtnes blacknes ingend • yd y thys pryncypell may denyed naturall phyloſophers ſo ſeyth wy whych whytenes thou may mys whytenes yf thou congele hyt ons thou haſt stone moſt preſyoſe stonys dry lyke moyſt dyd putrefy whych cauſyd color blacknes appere ryght ſo moyſt congelyd dry ingendryth whytenes ſhyneyng myght ſull clere drynes procedyth whytyth matter lyke blackyng moyſture doth hym ſhow color varyante aye new new cauſe thys y hett moſt temperate workyng mevyng mater contynually thereby alſo mater y alterate inward outward ſubſtancyally doth folys ſyght ſophyſtycally every parte fyre endure fluxybly fyxe ſtabull tyncture phyſycke determyneth eche dygeſtyon fyrſt stomack whych y drynes cauſyng whytnes wythout queſtyon lyke ſecond dygeſtyon cauſyth rednes complet lyver hete temperatnes ſo stone drynes hete dygeſtyd y whyte red complete thou muſt another ſecret knowe phyloſophers chyld ayre y borne beſy thee faſt cole blowe take nether mock skorne truſt truly elſe thy work y forlorne wythout thyne erth wyth water revyvyd trew congelyng ſhalt thou never ſee ſowle betwyxt hevyn erth beyng aryſyng fro erth ayre wyth water pure cauſyng lyfe every lyvely thyng inceſſably runnyng uppon foreſayd nature enforſyng better wyth hys cure whych ayre y fyre phyloſophy namyd oyle water myſtyly thus mene ayre whych oyle water call fyre oyntment spryte stone whych one thyng grownd wyſdomes goyth nether yn alone nether fyer water anone fyrſt yt outeledyth bryngyth yt yn water water whych wyll lyghtly twyn ſo may water water meve whych mevyng cauſyth deth lyfe water doth kyndly water cleve wythout repugnance ſtryfe whych water folys y nothyng ryfe beyng kynd wythowten dowte spryte callyd water leder owte water y ſecret lyfe every thyng y ſubſtance thys world found water eche thyng hath begynnyng ſhowyth woman ſhe ſhallbe unbound water whych paſſyth afore ſound callyd albyen fyrſt rennyng wyth grevoſe throwys afore ther chyldyng truly y cauſe pryncypall phyloſophers chargyd u pacyent tyll tyme water dryed powder wyth nurryſhyng hete contynuall vyolent qualytes contrarious every element tyll black whyte made unyon forever congelyd wythout dyvyſyon furthermore preparacion thys converſyon fro thyng thyng fro one ſtate another y done kyndly deſcrete operacion nature y sperme wythin mother sperme hete syſter brother whych converted wythin themſelf nature accion paſſyon laſt parfyt man bodely part nature whych y conſumate man y ſuch begynner whych though yt thus fro thyng thyng alterat owt kynd menge kynds dyd yt pa ſo mater ſpermatycall wythin one glas wythin hyt ſelfe muſt turne fro thyng thyng hete moſt temperate hyt noryſhyng another example naturall may thee tell ſubſtance egg nature y wrought chyk paſyng ſhell playner example cowd thought converſions made tyll forth brought fro ſtate ſtate lyke lyke yn kynd wyth nurryſhyng hete bere thys yn mynd another example may alſo rede vegetable thyngs takyng conſyderacyon every plant growyth hys owne ſede thorow moyſture naturall operacyon therefore mineralls nurryſhyd mynyſtracyon moyſture radycall whych theyr begynnyng paſſiyng theyer kynd wythin one glas turne fro thyng thyng agayne ther moder water go whych pryncyple unknowen thou laboureſt vayne y sperme thyngs ther mo kynd wyth kynd number two male female agent pacyent wythin matryce erth moſt oryent theſe turnyd hete fro thyng thyng wythin one glas ſo fro ſtate ſtate tyll tyme nature bryng one ſubſtance water regenerate ſo sperme wythin hys kynde y alterate abyll lykenes hys kynde multeplye doth kynde thyngs naturally tyme thys ſeyde proceſſe naturall whyle sperme conſevyd y growyng ſubſtance y nurryſhed wyth hys owne menſtruall whych water erth dyd bryng whoſe colour y greene fyrſt ſhowing tyme son hydyth hys lyght taking hys courſe thorow owte north nyght ſeyd menſtrue y ſay councell blod grene lyon vytrioll dame venus trewth thys tell thy begynnyng councell yf thou call thys ſecret y hyd phyloſophers grete ſmall whych blode drawen owte ſeyd lyon lac hete perfyt dygeſtyon thys blode ſecret menſtruall wherewyth sperme y nurryſhed temperatly y turnyd fecys corporall becom whyte perfytly dry congelyd fyxyd hys owne body bruſtyn blod ſyght yt may well ſeme thys warke namyd mylke whyte dyademe underſtonde fyery water thus acuate called menſtruall water wherein erth y loſyd naturally calcenat congelacyon may never twyne yet congele water thou may blyn thre part acuate water ſeyd afore wyth 4th part erth congelyd unto ſubſtance therefore ſo congelat fowerth part put water cryſtallyn make together dyſponſat congelacyon myner metallyne whych lyke ſworde new ſlypyd wyll ſhyne blacknes whych fyrſt wyll ſhowe fowerth parte geve yt water new mo inbybycyons many muſt yett geve yt ſecond thyrd alſo ſeyd proportyon kepe well thy wyt another fowerth tyme loke thou go fyfth tyme ſyxth paſſe fro put two part eche tyme three ſeventh tyme fyve part let bee thou haſt made thus ſeven tymes inbybycion ageyne muſt thow turne thy whele putrefy matter wythowte addycyon fyrſt blackneſſe abydyng yf thow wylt well whytenes congele yt eche dele rednes sowth aſſend haſt thou brought thy baſe unto end thus y thy water devydyd partyes two wyth fyrſt party body putryfycat thyne inbybycions ſecond part muſt go wyth whych matter y afterwards denygrat ſone uppon eſy decoccyon albyfycate yt y namyd phyloſophers sterry stone bryng rednes y ſyxth gate woon cibation ſeventh gate cibacion turne pen wryte syth yt muſt ſeventh place occupye word yt wylbe expedyte take tent therto underſtond wyttyly cibacion y callyd fedyng matter dry wyth mylke mete whych moderatly tyll yt brought thyrd order unto geve yt ſo much thou hyt glut beware dropſy alſo noyes flood lyttyll lyttyll therfore thou hyt put mete drynke ſemyth hyt good watry humor overgrow blood drynke therfore let hyt meſuryd ſo kyndly appetyte thou never quench therfro yf yt drynke much muſt yt vomyte ell wyll yt ſyk long fro dropſy therfore thy wombe thou ſave fro flux ell wyll hyt wrong whych rather lat yt thyrſt drynke amonge thou ſhold geve yt overmuch ons whych muſt youth dyattyd nons yf thou dyatt hyt nature doth requyre moderatly tyll hyt growen age fro cold hyt kepyng nurryſhyng wyth moyſt fyre ſhall yt grow wax full corrage thee pleſure advauntage ſhall make darke body hole bryght clenſyng theyer leproſenes thorow hys myght thre tymes thus muſt thou turne thy whele abowte kepyng rewle ſeyd cibacyon ſone yt fyre doth fele lyke wax yt wylbe redy unto lyquacyon thys chapter nedyth longer proteſtacion told thee dyatory moſt convenyent thyne element made equypolent alſo thou whytnes ſhalt bryng thy gold moſt lyke fygure lenys hawthorn tre callyd magneſya afore told whyte sulfur wythowte conbuſtebyllyte whych fro fyer away wyll never fle thus ſeventh gate thow deſyred▪ upſpryng son y conqueryd sublimation eight gate sublimacion word two ſpeke whych eyghth gate y folys sublyme sublyme thou ſo sublyme lyke wy sublyme trewly therfore thou ſhall mys thou make thy body firſt ſpirituall thy spyryts tought corporall som mercury vitriall salt ſublyme ſpryts fro scale yern steele fro eggſhells calcynyd quyk lyme theyer manner hyt sublyme ryght well ſuch sublymyng accordyth never adele entent sublyme ſo trewe sublymyng therfore wyll go sublymacyon fyrſt beware one thyng thou sublyme top thy veſſell without vyolence thou ſhalt yt downe bryng ageyne yt wyll abyde dwell hyt rejoyſyth wyth refrygeracion tell kepe hyt therfore wyth temperat hete adowne full forty dayes tyll hyt wex black abowen sowle begynnyth com owte fro hys owne vaynys ſubtyll y wyll wyth spryts aſſend withouten dowte bere thy mynde therfore thynke thys eclypſyd byn thy body putrify sublymyng water tyll bore thus ther venom ſpowtyd water black yt doth appeare become ſpirituall every dele withoute dowte sublymyng eſyly manner water doth hym bere ayre one chyld thus muſt bore water ageyne ſeyd theſe sublymacyon continuall laboryd ſo wyth hete moyſt temperate y whyte purely made ſpirituall hevyn uppon erth muſt reitterate unto sowle wyth body reincorporate erth becom afore hevyn whych wyll done sublymacyons ſevyn sublymacyon make cauſys thre fyrſt cauſe y make body spirituall ſecond spryt may corporall becom fyx wyth hyt ſubſtancyall thyrd cauſe y fro hys fylth orygynall may clenſyd hys fatnys ſulphuryoſe mynyſhyd hym whych y infectuoſe thus togeder depuryd wyll sublyme whyter snow ſyght wyll gretly comfort anon parfytly ſhalt thou know thy sprytts ſhall ſo downe throw thys gate ſhalbe unlockyd thys gate many one ſhyt mockyd fermentation ninth gate trew fermentacyon worker underſtond ſecrett therfore wyll expounde travelyd trewly thorow many lond ever myght fynde cold tell hyt yet god wolde evermore bleſſed laſt cum knowledge therof parfyt take heede therfore therof wryte fermentyng dyvers maners y whych medcyns muſt perpetuate clere water ſom leſyth son mone wyth ther medcyns makyth congelate whych fyer tyme examynate may abyde alter wyth complement ſuch ferment y intent yet kyndly ſom men fermentyng theyer medcynes thys wyſe mercury dyſſolvyng son mone wyth spryts tyll tyme wyll aryſe sublymyng together twyſe thryſe fermentacyon therof make y way yet hyt forſake som ther whych hath hap touch trothe parte fermentyng amalgam ther body wyth mercury lyke papp theruppon ther medcyns relentyng theſe secretts ſom hentyng trewth wyth parfyt complement becauſe nether putrefy alter ther ferment poynt therfore wyll dyſcloſe thee looke thou dydyſt wyth thy unparfyt body ſo wyth thy parfyt body every degre y ſey fyrſt thou putrefye prymary qualytes deſtroying utterly thys y wholey entent fyrſt thou alter thou ferment thy compound make ferment fowerth parte whych ferment son mone thou therfore maſter thys arte thy fermentacion lat thys done fyx water erth together ſone medcyn wax doth flowe uppon malgams loke thou hyt throw together y myxyd thy glaſſe well cloſyd make thy fyre ſo contenew hyt tyll fyxid well fermented deſyre make projeccyon thy pleaſure y medcyn ech dele parfyt thus muſt ferment red whyte lyke flower whete made paſt requyreth ferment whych leven call bred yt may kyndly taſt becom fode man woman moſt cordyall ryght ſo thy medcyn ferment thou ſhall yt may taſt wyth ferment pure aſſays evermore endure underſtond ther ferment three two body nature clene whych muſt altryd told thee thyrd moſt ſecret whych mene y fyrſt erth hys owne water grene therfore lyon doth thurſt make hym drynke tyll hys belly burſt thys queſtyon yf ſhold meve aske worker y thys thyng anon therby ſholde preve yf knowledge fermentyng many man ſpekyth wyth wondreng robyn hode bow whych never ſhot therin trow fermentacion trew tell y sowle wyth body incorporacyon reſtoryng hyt kyndly ſmell wyth taſt color naturall conſpyſacyon thyngs spryts abyde wyth body ſtedfaſtly wyth fyrſt confyxat proportionably body techyth spryt ſuffer fyer spryt body endure thy deſyre therfore thy gold wyth gold thou muſt ferment wyth hys owne water thyne erth clenſyd mene ell ſay element wyth element spryts lyfe goyng betweene lyke adamand thow haſt ſene yern hym draw ſo doth erth kynde draw downe hym hys sowle borne wyth wynd wyth mynd therfore thy sowle lede meng gold wyth gold ſay make element wyth element together ryn tyme fyre ſuffer may erth y ferment wythouten nay water water erth unto fermentacion thys wyſe muſt erth y gold ſo y sowle aſured ageyne hys mortal fone hath thys poſceſſion schal ſuffer povert ne non indygens treſour plente foyſon every man ſchal hym reverence non enemy ſchal hym non offence fro thi hondes gone pleyne gyf thow wilt thy parte y none abrayde ſtone wych thow haſt forlore alle reſon thow ſchuldys ben ſad thi hert nothyng glad chorle tel device eyred bred ſwite paradyce mo namys ſchal tel ſtone cal jagownce hys vertuis hys ſmel ben ſo ſwete ſo odeferus wyth ennock ely hath ſervis ſwete ſonge ſowndeth ſo ſcherpe wyth angelles voyſe paſſeth eny harpe nigrum deamond y morienis ſees white charbonkkel rolleth wave ſetryne reby ryche degree paſſeth ſtonys comen ſawe lapidery y grown olde lawe paſſeth ſtonys y hevyn cowrſe kynde planet ſevyn hyt y none chorle ſchuch treſour exſedeth alle stonys lapidery alle vertuis bereth flowr wyth joy grace yt maketh man mery thys worlde ſchal never byn ſory chorle thow paſſeth thy gras leberte even clerkys fyndeth bybell paradys yatis whan caſt angel fayr ſtyll downe kyng elyſawnder ther threſt ſtonys yt leſt soche ſtonys place ben brought soroful y chorle hevy hys thowte chorle yt tel thow wolt take hede byrde ermes y name worlde y ſo wyde wyth gletering grace every ſyde hoſe myght hys covertowr wer rychcher eny emperowr elyſawnder conquerowr ston ſmot downe upon hys helme whan hyt pyght mor peſe y ſo rownde hyt ther manys ſyght leyde ſo pleyne manly knyght tel wyth melde stevyn thys myghty grace cam owte fro hevyn hit cawſeth love maketh men gracius favorabel ever mannes ſyght hit maketh acorde two folk envyus comforteth sorowful maketh hevy herts lyght lyke paſſyng colur sunny bryght fole tel onys teche chorle pryce precious stony • men ſchalle put precius margareyt rubeys saferys odther stonys ynde emeraudys rownde perlys whyte byfore rude swyne love draffe kynde sowe delyteth hyr fynde mor fowle draffe hyr pygges glad al perry come owte granad heche thyng drawes hys ſemblable fyſſhes see beſtys stronde eyr fowlys y commendabyl plowghman tyll hys londe chorle mukforke hys honde leſe tyme eny tare tell bewar lapidare thow haddeſt thow getyſt thi lyme twygges panters defie let gon thow fowle ſeen leſe richches folye fre ſyng fle vvher lyſt fole goth large maketh hymſelfe thrall vviſdome thi • neres halfe defe like naſſe lyſteth upon harpe thow muſt go pype ive leffe better y ſyng thornes ſcharpe cage wyth chorle carpe hyt ſeyd folkes many yere agone chorles chorle • oft wo • gone chorle tolde vertuys wyth grete experience hyt ſume man better golde yt y fructius ſentence chepys croke y better launce adew globb • wyth herte ſore chorles clowchys com never chorle felt hys herte part tweyne ſorow ſunder ryve ala quod may wel wepe pleyne wreche never lyke thryve indure povert lyve foly wylfulnes loſt holy ryches lorde crye owte fortune grete treſor late keepyng wych myght made long contune wyth ilke stone levyd kyng yf ſet hyt ryng borne upon gode nowe ſchuld mor gon plowe whan byrd ſaw chorle thus morne hevy hys chere sche take flyght agayne returne toward hym ſayd ye ſchal dull chorle wiſdom lere taute y lefe byhynde reyſed awey clene owte thy meynde taw tey thys wyſdome ſentens every tale brought new haſtyle gyf ther credens unto tyme thow know hit trew y gold ſcheweth goldys hew ſtonys nature fynde byn saferus ſchewyth colour ynde thys doctryne loſt labour teche ſuch proverbys ſubſtaunce mayſt thow ſee thy lewd blynde error body poyſed balans weyth nounce lewde y thi remembraunce yet mor poyſe cloſyd myne entrayle body ſet countervayle body weyth unce myght ſton poyſeth mor doth grete jagounce thy brayne y dull thi witte almoſt gon hre wyſdomys thow haſt loſt thow ſchulds ſentence every tale gefe haſtyly credence badde alſo bewar even morowe thynge loſt ſuden adventur thow ſchulds make moche ſorow whan thow ſeyſt thow mayſt hit recover thow fayleſt wych doth thy beſy cure ſnare catch agayne thow art fole thy labor y vayne thyrde alſo thow doſt rave bad thow ſchulds maner wyſe covet thyng wych thow mayſt wych thow haſt fogetyn myne empryſe thaty may ſay playnly devyſe thow haſt madnes forgetyn thre notabyl wyſdomys taute hit wer foly mor wyth carpe teche wyſdomys mor leſſe holde hym madde bryngs forth hys harpe theron teche rode doilyd aſſe mad y ſyngyth fole maſſe y moſt madd doth hys beſyneſſe teche chorle termys gentleneſſe ſemeblabilly apryll may whan gentyl byrd moſt make melody cockow ſyng butoo lay odthir tewnys ſche hath fanteſy thus every thyng clerk ſpecify frute tree folke every age fro whenſe come tallage wynter tretyth hys welſom wyndys good sylver fyne purſe myne elſewhere make malliable el hold falſe unſtable amonges folke ever appere poudre coſt deere shall make good cauſe connyng ſhewe ſhall voydeth man let therout ſhette dore whyles ben privetie man u eſpy whyles werken philoſophye al bade fulfylled indede ylke ſervant anon yede maiſter ſhette dore anon labour ſpedily gone preeſt curſed chanons byddyng uppon fyre anon ſet thyng blewe fyre beſyed ful faſte chanon croſlet caſte pouder wherof ymade either chalke erthe glaſſe ſomwhat el worthe fly blynde preeſt bade hye theſe cole couchen al croſſlet token love quod chanon thyn hondes two shal werke al thing ſhalbe graunt mercy quod preeſt ful glad couched cole chanon bad whyle beſy fendely wretch falſe chanon foule fende fetche boſome toke bechen cole ful ſubtelly made hole therein put sylver lymayle unce ſtopped without fayle hole waxe kepe limayle underſtandeth falſe gyn made made byfore thynges ſhall tell herafter whiche brought er came begyle thought ſo er went twynne till turned coulde blynne dulleth whan ſpeke falſe hede fayne wolde wreke wyſte ſo varyaunt bydeth taketh heed syrs nowe godds love toke cole ſpake honde bare prively whyles preeſt couched beſily cole told er chanon ſayd frende ye done amys couched ought ſone ſhall amend quod nowe let medle therwith whyle pyte saint gyle ye ben right hotte ſe wel ye ſwete clothe wype away wete preest wyped hace chanon toke cole ſhrewe face layd aboven uppon mydwarde croſlet blewe wel afterwarde till cole gonne faſte brenne nowe yeve u drinke quod chanon ſwythe al ſhall wel undertake sytte downe let u mery make whan chanons bechen cole brent al limayle hole croſlet anon fell adoun ſoe muſt needes reſoun sen ſo even couched thereof wyſte preeſt nothing ala demed cole lyche goode ſleyght nothing underſtoode whan alkamiſtre ſawe tyme ryſeth syr preeſt quod ſtondeth byme wott well yngot none gothe walketh forth brynge chalke ſtone wol make ſame ſhappe yngott may happe bring eke bolle panne full water ſhall ſe thanne beſyneſſe ſhall happe preve yet ye ſhall misbyleve ne wronge conceyte abſence wol ben preſence goe come yon agayne chamber dore ſhortly ſayne opened ſhette went forth wey forthe carryed key comen agen withouten delay ſhulde tarry long day toke chalke ſhope wyſe yngot ſhall devyſe ſay toke owne ſleve teyne sylver yvel mote cheve unce weight taketh heed curſed
